MARGIN:0px" align=center><br></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:96px; FLOAT:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Item 1.01.</b></font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</b></font></p> <p style="CLEAR:left; MARGIN:0px"><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>On July 20, 2015 (the <font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial Unicode MS,Times New Roman">&#147;</font><b><i>Closing Date</i></b><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial Unicode MS,Times New Roman">&#148;</font>), Blue Calypso, Inc., a Delaware corporation &nbsp;(&#147;<b><i>Blue</i></b> <b><i>Calypso</i></b>&#148;), Blue Calypso Holdings, Inc. (&#147;<b><i>Holdings</i></b>&#148;), Blue Calypso, LLC (&#147;<b><i>LLC</i></b>&#148;) and Blue Calypso Latin America, S.A. (&#147;<b><i>Blue Latin</i></b>&#148; and together with Holdings and Blue Latin, the<b><i> </i></b>&#147;<b><i>Subsidiaries,</i></b>&#148; and together with Blue Calypso, collectively, the &#147;<b><i>Company</i></b>&#148;) entered into a Note Purchase Agreement (the &#147;<b><i>Note Purchase Agreement</i></b>&#148;) with an institutional investor (the &#147;<b><i>Lender</i></b>&#148;), pursuant to which the Company sold to the Lender a senior convertible note in the aggregate principal amount of $550,000 (the &#147;<b><i>Note</i></b>&#148;) for a purchase price of $500,000 payable to the Company by the Lender.</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>The Note is due on July 20, 2016 (the &#147;<b><i>Maturity Date</i></b>&#148;). On January 17, 2016 (the &#147;<b><i>Guaranteed Interest Date</i></b>&#148;), the Company shall be obligated to pay the Lender interest equal to 10% of the then Principal outstanding on the Guaranteed Interest Date. At any time following the Guaranteed Interest Date, the Note, including all accrued but unpaid interest, default interest and any applicable late charges thereon, shall be convertible at the option of the Lender, at a conversion price equal to $7.6335 per share. The Note may be prepaid at any time by the Company (i) in shares of common stock of the Company at a 20% discount to the average of the three daily volume weighted average prices of Blue Calypso&#146;s common stock for the prior three trading days (the &#147;<b><i>Prepayment Price</i></b>&#148;), provided the Company is then and for a period prior thereto is in compliance with the Equity Conditions and/or (ii) in cash at a 120% premium to the amount then outstanding.</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>If the $550,000 principal amount of the Note and all accrued but unpaid interest thereof is not paid in full on or before January 16, 2016, the Note shall amortize in four equal payments payable on January 20, 2016, February 20, 2016, March 20, 2016 and April 20, 2016. These payments shall be paid (i) in cash at a 120% premium, and/or (ii) in shares of Blue Calypso&#146;s common stock at the Prepayment Price, provided Blue Calypso is in compliance with the Equity Conditions (as defined in the Note). </p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>If the Company effectuates a registered public offering pursuant to which the Company receives gross proceeds of no less than $5,000,000 (a &#147;<b><i>Qualified Public Offering</i></b>&#148;), 50% of the amount then outstanding under the Note shall convert into such Qualified Public Offering at a 20% discount to the price paid by investors in such Qualified Public Offering. The remaining 50% balance of the amount then outstanding under Note shall be paid in cash at a 120% premium to the amount then due from the proceeds of the Qualified Public Offering.</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>The Note contains certain limitations on conversion including, but not limited to, no conversion is permitted if, after giving effect to the conversion, the Lender would beneficially own in excess of 4.99% of the Company&#146;s outstanding shares of Common Stock or 9.99% at the option of such Buyer. </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px" align=justify>&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>The Note and the Note Purchase Agreement imposes penalties on the Company for, among other items, any failure to timely deliver any shares of its Common Stock issuable upon conversion and any failure to satisfy the current public information requirements under Rule 144(c) of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#147;<b><i>Securities Act</i></b>&#148;). &nbsp;The Note also contains a variety of Events of Default (as defined in the Note) including, but not limited to failures to </p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px" align=center>2</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px><br></p> <p style=MARGIN:0px><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always; MARGIN:0px" align=justify>repay amounts when due under the Note and instances of Blue Calypso&#146;s common stock trading below certain levels as defined under the Note. </p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>The descriptions of the Note Purchase Agreement and Note set forth above are not complete, and are qualified in their entirety by reference to the full text of such agreements that are attached as exhibits to this Report. Readers should review these agreements for a more complete understanding of the terms and conditions of such agreements.</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:96px; FLOAT:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><b>Item 2.03.</b></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; PADDING-LEFT:96px; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px" align=justify><b>Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</b></p> <p style="CLEAR:left; MARGIN:0px" align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify>The information required to be disclosed under this Item 2.03 is set forth above under Item 1.01.</p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify>&nbsp;</p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:96px; FLOAT:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Item 3.02.</b></font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Unregistered Sale of Equity Securities.</b></font></p> <p style="CLEAR:left; MARGIN:0px" align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>On July 20, 2015, the Company issued the Note described in Item 1.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-K in exchange for gross proceeds of $500,000. The details of this transaction, are disclosed in Item 1.01, which is incorporated by reference into this Item 3.02.</font></p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>Maxim Group LLC acted as placement agent on the transaction and received a fee of $38,500.</font></p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>The issuance of the Note was not registered under the Securities Act or the securities laws of any state, and was offered and sold in reliance upon the exemption from registration under the Securities Act pursuant to exemptions from such registration requirements provided by Section 4(a)(2) and/or Regulation D (Rule 506) under the Securities Act.</font></p> <p style=MARGIN:0px align=justify><br></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:96px; FLOAT:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Item 9.01</b></font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff><b>Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></font></p> <p style="CLEAR:left; MARGIN:0px" align=justify><br></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:48px; FLOAT:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>10.1</font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; PADDING-LEFT:48px; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>Form of Note Purchase Agreement dated as of July 20, 2015 by and between the Lender, Blue Calypso, Inc., Blue Calypso Holdings, Inc., Blue Calypso, LLC and Blue Calypso Latin America, S.A.</font></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; WIDTH:48px; FLOAT:left; CLEAR:left; MARGIN-TOP:0px"><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>10.2</font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0px; TEXT-INDENT:-2px" align=justify><font style=BACKGROUND-COLOR:#ffffff>Form of Senior Convertible Note issued on July 20, 2015</font></p> <p style="CLEAR:left; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Lender</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), BLUE CALYSO, INC., a Delaware corporation (together with all of its successors and current and future, direct and/or indirect Subsidiaries, collectively, the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Borrower</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), BLUE CALYPSO HOLDINGS, INC., a Texas corporation (&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Holdings</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), BLUE CALYPSO, LLC, a Texas limited liability company (&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Blue Latin </font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;, and together with Holdings, LLC and each of such persons successors current and future, direct or indirect, wholly owned or partially owned Subsidiaries, collectively, (the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in" align=justify><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>THE PARTIES HERETO agree as follows:</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>ARTICLE 1.</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>DEFINITIONS</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in">&nbsp;</p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:1px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 1.01.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Defined Terms</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; In addition to terms defined elsewhere in this Agreement or any Supplement or Exhibit hereto, when used herein, the following terms shall have the following meanings:</font></p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 6pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in" align=justify><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>1933 Act</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder.</font></p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 6pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in" align=justify><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>1934 Act</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:115%" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Affiliate</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean any Person which, directly or indirectly, owns or controls, on an aggregate basis, a ten (10%) percent or greater interest in any other Person, or which is controlled by or is under common control with any other Person. </font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Business Day</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean any day other than a Saturday or Sunday or any other day on which the Federal Reserve Bank of New York is not open for business.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Closing</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean the time of issuance and sale by the Borrower of the $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note to the Lender for the $500,000 Purchase Price on the Closing Date. </font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Closing Date</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean the date the $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note is purchased by the Lender from the Borrower for the $500,000 Purchase Price pursuant to this Agreement.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>Contingent Obligation</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#148; shall mean as to any Person, any direct or indirect liability, contingent or otherwise, of that Person with respect to any indebtedness, lease, dividend or other obligation of another Person if the primary purpose or intent of the Person incurring such liability, or the primary effect thereof, is to provide assurance to the obligee of such liability that such liability will be paid or discharged, or that any agreements relating thereto will be complied with, or that the holders of such liability will be protected (in whole or in part) against loss with respect thereto.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in">&nbsp;</p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; and paralegals&#146; fees or charges relating to the preparation of the Documents and the enforcement of Lender&#146;s rights, remedies and powers under this Agreement, the Note and/or the other Documents, including, but not limited to, the drafting of any documents and the preparation and enforcement of this Agreement and the other Documents.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; of the assets of such Person will, as of such date, exceed the amount of all &#147;liabilities of such Person, contingent or otherwise&#148;, as of such date, as such quoted terms are determined in accordance with applicable federal and state laws governing determinations of the insolvency of debtors, (ii)&nbsp;the present fair saleable value of the assets of such Person will, as of such date, be greater than the amount that will be required to pay the liability of such Person on its debts as such debts become absolute and matured, (iii)&nbsp;such Person will not have, as of such date, an unreasonably small amount of capital with which to conduct its business, and (iv)&nbsp;such Person will be able to pay its debts as they mature.&nbsp; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>provided&nbsp;</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> that (i) no Event of Default or event that with the passage of time or the giving of notice, or both, would become an Event of Default shall have occurred or would result therefrom; and (ii) the conditions in </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Section 5.01</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> have been satisfied.&nbsp; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 2.3.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Note</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Loan shall be evidenced by the $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note. </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Purchase Price and Payment of the Purchase Price for the Notes</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Purchase Price for the $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note shall be $500,000 in the aggregate, representing an original issue discount of $50,000.&nbsp; On the Closing Date, the Lender shall pay the Borrower the $500,000 Purchase Price (less (i) all of the Lender&#146;s Expenses (as defined below), and (ii) the Maxim Placement Fee (as defined below), for the $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note by wire transfer of immediately available funds to the Borrower in accordance with the Borrower&#146;s written wiring instructions, against delivery of the duly executed $550,000 aggregate principal amount Note.&nbsp; </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:2px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 2.5.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Lender&#146;s Cost and Expenses</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; On the Closing Date, all direct and indirect reasonable out-of-pocket costs and expenses of the Lender related to the negotiation, due diligence, preparation, closing, and all other items regarding and/or related to the Documents and all of the transactions contemplated herein and therein, including, but not limited to, $27,500, which shall be payable to the Lender&#146;s legal counsel plus such legal counsel&#146;s documented expenses (collectively, the </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Lender&#146;s Expenses</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), shall be due and payable from the Borrower to the Lender (less $10,000 previously paid); and the Lender shall subtract from the $500,000 Purchase Price to be paid to the Borrower for the $550,000 aggregate principal amount of the Note, all of Lender&#146;s Expenses and the Lender shall pay on the Closing Date to the Lender&#146;s counsel the fees and expenses set forth above in immediately available funds by wiring such funds to Lender&#146;s counsel pursuant to wiring instructions provided to the Lender by its legal counsel.&nbsp; Notwithstanding anything to the contrary, without the consent of Borrower, neither the Lender nor its counsel shall incur any expenses that the Borrower is liable for, except lien, judgment, tax and related searches which were approved by the Borrower, and which such other expenses shall not exceed in the aggregate $1,500.&nbsp; Although the Lender&#146;s Expenses in an amount not to exceed, without the consent of the Borrower, $29,000 (which includes the actual costs of the lien, judgment and tax searches) are being subtracted by the Lender from the Purchase Price actually delivered to the Borrower, such Lender&#146;s Expenses shall constitute part of the Purchase Price and shall not directly and/or indirectly reduce and or result in any set-off the aggregate principal amount of the Note or result in a set-off and/or reduction of any other funds owed by the Borrower to the Lender. </font></p><a name=_aciFooter7> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; and/or (3) any agreement binding upon Borrower or any of Borrower&#146;s properties except as would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect, and (v) do not result in, or require, the creation or imposition of any Lien and/or encumbrance on any of Borrower&#146;s properties or revenues pursuant to any law, rule, regulation or ordinance or otherwise.&nbsp; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Except as disclosed in the Public Reports, the Borrower maintains a system of internal accounting controls sufficient to provide reasonable assurance that (i)&nbsp;transactions are executed in accordance with management&#146;s general or specific authorizations, (ii)&nbsp;transactions are recorded as necessary to permit preparation of financial statements in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles and to maintain asset and liability accountability, (iii)&nbsp;access to assets or incurrence of liabilities is permitted only in accordance with management&#146;s general or specific authorization and (iv)&nbsp;the recorded accountability for assets and liabilities is compared with the existing assets and liabilities at reasonable intervals and appropriate action is taken with respect to any difference.&nbsp; Except as disclosed in the Public Reports, the Borrower maintains disclosure controls and procedures (as such term is defined in Rule&nbsp;13a-15 under the 1934 Act) that are effective in ensuring that information required to be disclosed by the Borrower in the reports that it files or submits under the 1934 Act is recorded, processed, summarized and reported, within the time periods specified in the rules&nbsp;and forms of the SEC, including, without limitation, controls and procedures designed to ensure that information required to be disclosed by the Borrower in the reports that it files or submits under the 1934 Act is accumulated and communicated to the Borrower&#146;s management, including its principal executive officer or officers and its principal financial officer or officers, as appropriate, to allow timely decisions regarding required disclosure.&nbsp; Except as disclosed in the Public Reports, during the twelve months prior to the date hereof the Borrower has not received any notice or correspondence from any accountant relating to any material weakness in any part of the system of internal accounting controls of the Borrower.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(ww)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Foreign Corrupt Practices</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. Neither the Borrower, nor any director, officer, agent, employee or other Person acting on behalf of the Borrower has, in the course of its actions for, or on behalf of, the Borrower (i) used any corporate funds for any unlawful contribution, gift, entertainment or other unlawful expenses relating to political activity; (ii) made any direct or indirect unlawful payment to any foreign or domestic government official or employee from corporate funds; (iii) violated or is in violation of any provision of the U.S. Foreign Corrupt Practices Act of 1977, as amended; or (iv) made any unlawful bribe, rebate, payoff, influence payment, kickback or other unlawful payment to any foreign or domestic government official or employee.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(xx)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Sarbanes-Oxley Act</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. The Borrower is in compliance with any and all applicable requirements of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002, as amended, that are effective as of the date hereof, and any and all applicable rules and regulations promulgated by the SEC thereunder that are effective as of the date hereof.</font></p><a name=_aciFooter15> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>14</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_16> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(yy)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Equity Capitalization</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. Borrower shall (i) maintain complete and accurate books and records; (ii) permit access by the Lender and its agents and/or representatives to such books and records as they relate to this Agreement, the Securities, and/or the other Documents; and (iii) permit such persons, upon two (2) days prior written notice, to inspect the properties, whether real or personal, and operations of Borrower.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; Borrower shall maintain such insurance as may be required by law and such other insurance to the extent and against such hazards and liabilities as is customarily maintained by companies similarly situated.&nbsp; All property insurance policies shall, within 30 days following the Security Start Date, contain lender loss payable clauses in form and substance reasonably satisfactory to the Lender, naming the Lender as a lender loss payee, mortgagee and/or additional insured, as its interest may appear, and providing that such policies and lender loss payable clauses may not be canceled, amended or terminated unless at least thirty (30) days (or ten (10) days in the case of non-payment of premiums) prior written notice thereof has been given to the Lender.&nbsp; All insurance proceeds received by the Lender may be retained by the Lender, in its sole discretion, for application to the payment of the Liabilities as the Lender may determine.&nbsp; </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; prior written notice before Borrower changes its name or does business under any other name.</font></p><a name=_aciFooter18> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; From and after the date of this Agreement through and including the date all of the Borrowers and each of its Subsidiaries&#146; Indebtedness and all other obligations owed to the Lender pursuant to the Documents, including, but not limited to, the Note is paid and performed in full, confirmation of which must be obtained by in writing from the Lender, the Borrower shall (a) issue or cause its Transfer Agent to issue the Conversion Shares and all other shares of Common Stock required to be issued to the Holder or its broker only (subject to the immediately following clause (b)), (b) issue or cause its Transfer Agent to issue shares of Common Stock to the Lender or its broker under the Note from sources other than the Reserve, unless the Lender delivers to the Borrower written pre-approval of such issuance from the Reserve, and (c) not reduce the Reserve under any circumstances, unless the Lender delivers to the Borrower written pre-approval of such reduction.&nbsp; The Borrower shall immediately add shares of Common Stock to the Reserve to ensure that the greater of (i) 509,000 shares of Common Stock and (ii) Required Reserve Amount (the greater of (i) and (ii) being the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; Notwithstanding to the contrary provided herein or elsewhere, if at any time the number of shares of Common Stock in the Reserve, is less than the Required Reserved Amount, the Lender may send written notice to the Borrower&#146;s then Transfer Agent to increase out of the Borrower&#146;s authorized but unissued shares of Common Stock such number of additional shares of Common Stock so the Reserve consists of at least the Required Reserve Amount, provided, that the number of shares of Common Stock in the Reserve shall never be decreased or used for any other purposes other than for issue to the Holder upon each conversion by the Holder of the Note into Conversion Shares.&nbsp; Until the date on which the Holder shall have sold all of the Interest Shares and Conversion Shares</font><b><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> </font></b><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>and none of the Notes are outstanding (the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Reporting Period</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), the Borrower shall timely file all reports required to be filed by the Borrower with the SEC pursuant to the 1934 Act within the time periods required by the SEC including all applicable extension periods, and the Borrower shall not terminate its status as an issuer required to file reports under the 1934 Act even if the 1934 Act or the rules&nbsp;and regulations thereunder would no longer require or otherwise permit such termination.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(p)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>The Documents</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Borrower and each of its Subsidiaries shall comply with all of their respective obligations under any of the Documents following the Closing Date.&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:5px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 4.02.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Negative Covenants</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Until all the Liabilities are paid in full, Borrower covenants and agrees that:</font></p><a name=_aciFooter21> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>20</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_22> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"><a name=_aciHeader22> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:right; MARGIN:0in 0in 10pt" align=right>&nbsp;</p></div><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(a)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Restricted Payments</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. The Borrower shall not directly or indirectly, redeem, defease, repurchase, repay or make any payments in respect of, by the payment of cash or cash equivalents (in whole or in part, whether by way of open market purchases, tender offers, private transactions or otherwise), all or any portion of any Indebtedness, whether by way of payment in respect of principal of (or premium, if any) or interest on, such Indebtedness, except for Permitted Indebtedness; </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>provided</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>however</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, that notwithstanding anything to the contrary provided herein or elsewhere (including the definition of Permitted Indebtedness), in no event shall the Borrower directly and/or indirectly make any payment to any officer, director, or 5% or greater beneficial holder of the Borrower&#146;s voting stock or Common Stock or an affiliate of the Borrower and/or any affiliate of any such person representing the direct and/or indirect repayment of Indebtedness, premiums and/or interest on Indebtedness, unpaid salaries, consulting fees, expenses, accrued but unpaid interest and/or otherwise; provided, that the Borrower may reimburse officers of Borrower for their reasonable out-of-pocket expenses incurred by such persons in connection with their employment with the Borrower in the ordinary course of business.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(b)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Restricted Issuances</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Borrower shall not, directly or indirectly, (i) issue any Securities and/or Indebtedness (other than as contemplated by this Agreement) or (ii) issue any other securities that would cause a breach or default and/or an Event of Default under the Note and/or any other Document.&nbsp; </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(c)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Restriction on Redemption and Dividends</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Borrower shall not, directly or indirectly, redeem, repurchase or declare or pay any dividend or distribution on any of its capital stock whether in cash, stock rights and/or property.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(d)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Restriction on Transfer of Assets</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. Neither the Borrower nor any of its Subsidiaries shall, directly or indirectly, sell, assign, transfer, spin-off, split-off, close, convey or otherwise dispose of any assets or rights of the Borrower owned or hereafter acquired whether in a single transaction or a series of related transactions&nbsp; (an &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>IP Transaction</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;).&nbsp; For purposes of clarity, an IP Transaction shall not include proceeds from licensing or settling any suits of infringement or any other proceeds derived from the normal course of business which do not include the sale or transfer of the IP assets.&nbsp; Notwithstanding anything to the contrary provided herein or elsewhere, in the event of an IP Transaction, the Borrower and each of its Subsidiaries shall after the payment of the legal fees and expenses owed to Fish &amp; Richardson (&#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>IP Counsel</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;) pursuant to the Letter Agreement by and between the Borrower and/or any of its Subsidiaries and IP Counsel executed by the Borrower on September 2, 2011 and by its IP Counsel on September 1, 2011 (the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>F&amp;R Letter</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;), pay to the Lender within five (5) Business Days of the date Borrower or any of its Subsidiaries shall receive proceeds from any IP Transaction, all sums owed to the Lender by the Borrower and/or any of its Subsidiaries pursuant to the Note and/or the other Documents; </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>provided</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>further</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, that (i) the F&amp;R Letter cannot be directly or indirectly modified, restated, terminated and another agreement entered into, supplemented amended and/or otherwise changed if the result thereof could result in IP Counsel directly and/or indirectly receiving more fees than those set forth in the originally executed F&amp;R Letter, (ii) IP Counsel shall not be paid, directly and/or indirectly any sums in excess of those stated in the originally executed F&amp;R Letter and/or (iii) neither the Borrower nor any Subsidiary shall take any action that could directly or indirectly adversely affect the right of the Lender to receive any IP Transaction proceeds for the payment of all obligations owed to the Lender by the Borrower and/or any of its Subsidiaries under and pursuant to the Note and the other Documents. All amounts owed to the Lender by the Borrower and/or any of its Subsidiaries shall be paid to the Lender in immediately available funds by wire transfer pursuant to wiring instructions provided to the Borrower from the Lender, and (iv) neither the Borrower, any of its Subsidiaries and/or any other person other than F&amp;R (and then only in the amounts set forth the originally executed F&amp;R Letter), shall be entitled to keep and/or use for any purpose (directly and/or indirectly), any IP Transaction proceeds until all Indebtedness and other obligations owed by the Borrower and/or any of its Subsidiaries to the Lender are paid in full.&nbsp; The Borrower shall give the Lender 15 day prior written notice of any such IP Transaction which notice </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>shall include a description of the IP Transaction, the Closing Date of the IP Transaction, the terms of the IP Transaction including all funds to be received by the Borrower and/or its Subsidiaries and a detailed account of the payments owed and to be paid to IP Counsel and to the Lender together with all IP Transaction documents, which IP Transaction documents shall include as a condition precedent to the closing of any IP Transaction, the payment of all funds owed to the Lender under this Agreement, the Note and the other Documents. </font></p><a name=_aciFooter22> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>21</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_23> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"><a name=_aciHeader23> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:right; MARGIN:0in 0in 10pt" align=right>&nbsp;</p></div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(e)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Change in Nature of Business</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp;The Borrower shall not, directly or indirectly, engage in any business substantially different from the business conducted by the Borrower on the Closing Date or any business substantially related or incidental thereto.&nbsp; The Borrower shall not, directly or indirectly, modify its or their corporate structure for any purpose.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(f)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Indebtedness</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not incur or permit to exist any Indebtedness, except for Permitted Indebtedness.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(g)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Liens</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not create or permit to exist any mortgage, pledge, title retention lien, or other lien, encumbrance or security interest with respect to any assets whether now owned or hereafter acquired and owned, except for Permitted Liens.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(h)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Guaranties, Loans or Advances</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not become or be a guarantor or surety of, or otherwise become or be responsible in any manner with respect to any undertaking of any other Person, or make or permit to exist any loans or advances to or investments in any other Person, except for the endorsement, in the ordinary course of collection, of instruments payable to it or to its order.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(i)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Violation of Law</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not violate any law, statute, ordinance, rule, regulation, judgment, decree, order, writ or injunction of any federal, state or local authority, court, agency, bureau, board, commission, department or governmental body, if any such violation could have a Material Adverse Effect.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(j)</font></p> <p style="PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Unconditional Purchase Obligations</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not enter into or be a party to any contract for the purchase of materials, supplies or other property or services if such contract requires that payment be made by it regardless of whether or not delivery is ever made of such materials, supplies or other property or services.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(k)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Use of Proceeds</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not permit any proceeds of the Loan to be used either directly or indirectly, for the purpose, whether immediate, incidental or ultimate, of &#147;purchasing or carrying any margin stock&#148; within the meaning of Regulation U of the Board of Governors of the Federal Reserve System, as amended from time to time.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(l)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Hedge Agreements</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not enter into any hedge agreement other than hedge agreements entered into in the ordinary course of business, and not for speculative purposes, to protect against changes in interest rates or foreign exchange rates. </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(m)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>ERISA</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Borrower shall not create or become obligated under any Plan.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(n)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>No Variable Rate Transactions, Etc.</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&nbsp; As long as any Principal, accrued but unpaid interest, Late Charges on the Note and/or in the other Documents is, outstanding, the Borrower shall not directly and/or indirectly (i)(I) consummate any exchange of any Indebtedness and/or securities of the Borrower for any other securities and/or Indebtedness of the Borrower, (II) cooperate with any person to effect any exchange of securities and/or Indebtedness of the Borrower in connection with a proposed sale of such securities from an existing holder of such securities to a third party), and/or (III) reduce and/or </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>otherwise change the exercise price, conversion price and/or exchange price of any Common Stock Equivalent of the Borrower and/or amend any non-convertible Indebtedness of the Borrower to make it convertible into securities of the Borrower, (ii) issue or sell any of its securities either (I) at a conversion, exercise or exchange rate or price that is based upon and/or varies with the trading prices of, or quotations for, the shares of Common Stock, and/or (II) with a conversion, exercise or exchange rate and/or price that is subject to being reset on one or more occasions either (x) at some future date after the initial issuance of such securities or (y) upon the occurrence of specified or contingent events directly or indirectly related to the business of the Borrower or the market for the Common Stock, and/or (iii) enter into any agreement (including, without limitation, an &#147;equity line of credit&#148; or an &#147;at-the-market offering&#148;) whereby the Borrower may sell securities at a future determined price.&nbsp; Any transaction contemplated in by </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Section 4.02(n)</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, shall be referred to as a &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Variable Rate Transaction</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&#148; The Lender shall be entitled to obtain injunctive relief against the Borrower to preclude any Variable Rate Transaction (without the need for the posting of any bond or similar item, which the Borrower hereby expressly and irrevocably waives the requirement for), which remedy shall be in addition to any right of the Lender to collect damages.</font></p><a name=_aciFooter23> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>22</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_24> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"><a name=_aciHeader24> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:right; MARGIN:0in 0in 10pt" align=right>&nbsp;</p></div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(o)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Transactions with Affiliates</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Except for such transactions described in the Public Reports, including any renewals or extensions thereof, the Borrower shall not directly and/or indirectly enter into, renew, extend or be a party to, any transaction or series of related transactions (including, without limitation, lending funds to an Affiliate and/or borrowing funds from any Affiliate, the purchase, sale, lease, transfer or exchange of property, securities or assets of any kind or the rendering of services of any kind) with any officer, director, Affiliate and/or any Affiliate of such person.</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>ARTICLE 5.</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>CLOSING CONDITIONS</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in">&nbsp;</p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; The Lender&#146;s obligation to enter into the Documents and purchase the Note is subject to the fulfillment of each and every one of the following conditions prior to or contemporaneously with the Lender entering into the Documents and purchasing the Note (unless waived by Lender in their sole and absolute discretion):</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(a)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; (d) all Closing Conditions set forth in Section 5.01 have been met by the Borrower of each Subsidiary, and (e) no event has occurred and/or that the Borrower anticipates occurring that (without regard for any action required to be taken by the Lender, (including, but not limited to, declaring an Event of Default and/or providing any notices) has resulted in an Event of Default or with the passage of time would result in an Event of Default.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Closing Conditions of Borrower</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The obligation of the Borrower to sell and issue the Note to the Lender at the Closing is subject to the fulfillment, to the Borrower&#146;s reasonable satisfaction, prior to or contemporary at the Closing, of each of the following conditions (unless waived by the Borrower): </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(a)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Representations and Warranties</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Each of the representations and warranties made by Lender in or pursuant to the Documents and all Schedules and/or Exhibits to this Agreement and/or any of the other Documents shall be true and correct in all material respects on and as of the Closing Date as </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>if made (or given) on and as of such date (except where such representation and warranty speaks of a specific date in which case such representation and warranty shall be true and correct as of such date). </font></p><a name=_aciFooter26> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>25</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_27> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"><a name=_aciHeader27> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:right; MARGIN:0in 0in 10pt" align=right>&nbsp;</p></div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US></p> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(b)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>No Injunction</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. No statute, regulation, order, decree, writ, ruling or injunction shall have been enacted, entered, promulgated, threatened in writing or endorsed by any court or governmental authority of competent jurisdiction which prohibits the consummation of or which would materially modify or delay any of the transactions contemplated by the Documents.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:95px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font size=3 style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>(c)</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Receipt of the $500,000 Purchase Price</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. The Borrower shall receive at the Closing, the $500,000 Purchase Price less the (i) Lender&#146;s Expenses, and (ii) the Maxim Placement Fee, all of which funds set forth in (i) and (ii) of this </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Section 5.02(c)</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, while constituting part of the $500,000 Purchase Price shall be paid directly to the Lender, the Lender&#146;s legal counsel and Maxim by the Lender without resulting in any set-off and/or reduction in the $550,000 aggregate principal amount of the Note and/or any set-off or reduction in any other Liabilities or amounts owed by the Borrower to the Lender.</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>ARTICLE 6.</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>MISCELLANEOUS</font></p> <p style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:avoid; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in">&nbsp;</p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:3px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 6.1.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>No Waiver; Modifications In Writing</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; No failure or delay on the part of Lender in exercising any right, power or remedy pursuant to the Documents shall operate as a waiver thereof, nor shall any single or partial exercise of any such right, power or remedy preclude any other or further exercise thereof, or the exercise of any other right, power or remedy.&nbsp; No amendment, modification, supplement, termination or waiver of any provision of the Documents, nor any consent by the Lender to any departure by Borrower therefrom, shall be effective unless the same shall be in writing and signed by the Lender.&nbsp; Any waiver of any provision of the Documents and any consent by the Lender to any departure by Borrower from the terms of any provision of the Documents shall be effective only in the specific instance and for the specific purpose for which given.&nbsp; No notice to or demand on Borrower in any case shall entitle Borrower to any other or further notice or demand in similar or other circumstances.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:7px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 6.2.</font></p> <p style="PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Set-Off</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; The Lender shall have the right to set-off, appropriate and apply toward payment of any of the Liabilities, in such order of application as the Lender may from time to time and at any time elect, any cash, credit, deposits, accounts, securities and any other property of Borrower which is in transit to or in the possession, custody or control of Lender, or any agent, bailee, or Affiliate of the Lender. Borrower hereby grants to Lender a security interest in all such property.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 6.3.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Notices</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>. All notices required or permitted hereunder shall be in writing and shall be deemed effectively given: (a) upon personal delivery to the party to be notified, (b) when sent by confirmed telex, facsimile or e-mail if sent during normal business hours of the recipient; if not, then on the next Trading Day, (c) five (5) days after having been sent by registered or certified mail, return receipt requested, postage prepaid, or (d) one (1) day after deposit with a nationally recognized overnight courier, specifying next day delivery, with written verification of receipt:</font></p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in">&nbsp;</p><a name=_aciFooter27> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>26</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_28> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in">&nbsp;</p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>If to Borrower:</font></p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in">&nbsp;</p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>BLUE CALYPSO, INC.</font></p> <p style="MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt 2.5in; TEXT-INDENT:-1.5in"><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>101 W. PADDING-RIGHT:0%"> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in">&nbsp;</p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 6.4.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Costs, Expenses and Taxes</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; Notwithstanding anything to the contrary provided herein or elsewhere, Borrower agrees to pay (A) on the Closing Date all of the Lender&#146;s Expenses; and (B) following the Closing Date, all fees and expenses incurred by the Lender (including, but not limited to, outside counsel to the Lender) in connection with the administration and enforcement of the Documents and/or and the Loan.&nbsp; In addition, Borrower shall pay any and all stamp, transfer and other similar taxes payable or determined to be payable in connection with the execution and delivery of the Documents agrees to hold the Lender harmless from and against any and all liabilities with respect to or resulting from any delay in paying or omission to pay such taxes.&nbsp; If any suit or proceeding arising from any of the foregoing is brought against the Lender, Borrower, to the extent and in the manner directed by Lender, will resist and defend such suit or proceeding or cause the same to be resisted and defended by counsel approved by Lender.&nbsp; If Borrower shall fail to do any act or thing which each has covenanted </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>and/or agreed to do under this Agreement and/or any other Document or any representation or warranty on the part of Borrower contained in this Agreement and/or any other Document shall be breached, the Lender may, in its sole and absolute discretion, do the same or cause it to be done or remedy any such breach, and may expend its funds for such purpose; and any and all amounts so expended by the Lender shall be repayable to the Lender by Borrower immediately upon the Lender&#146;s demand therefor, with interest at a rate equal to ten (10%) percent during the period from and including the date funds are so expended by the Lender to the date of repayment in full, and any such amounts due and owing to the Lender shall be deemed to be part of the Liabilities secured hereunder and under the other Documents. The obligations of Borrower under this </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Section 6.4</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>shall survive the termination of this Agreement and the discharge of the other obligations of Borrower under the Documents.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; FONT-SIZE:12pt; HEIGHT:9px; WIDTH:151px; FLOAT:left; PADDING-BOTTOM:0px; MARGIN-TOP:0px; TEXT-INDENT:48px"><font style=FONT-SIZE:11pt>Section 6.5.</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0in"></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US><u>Indemnity, Etc</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; In addition to the payment of expenses pursuant to </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Section 6.4</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>, whether or not all and/or any of the transactions contemplated hereby shall be consummated, Borrower agrees to indemnify, pay and hold Lender, and each of such Lender&#146;s assignees and affiliates and their respective officers, directors, employees, agents, consultants, auditors, and attorneys of any of them (collectively called the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Indemnities</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;) harmless from and against any and all liabilities, obligations, losses, damages, penalties, actions, judgments, suits, claims, costs, expenses and disbursements of any kind or nature whatsoever (including the reasonable fees and disbursements of counsel for such Indemnitees in connection with any investigative, administrative or judicial proceeding commenced or threatened, whether or not such Indemnitee shall be designated a party thereto) that may be imposed on, incurred by, or asserted against that Indemnitee, in any manner relating to or arising out of the SEC Reports, this Agreement and/or the other Documents, the consummation of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and the other Documents, the statements contained in any term sheet delivered by the Lender, the Lender&#146;s agreement to make the Loan, the use or intended use of the proceeds of the Loan or the exercise of any right or remedy hereunder or under the other Documents (the &#147;</font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>Indemnified Liabilities</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>&#148;); </font><u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>provided&nbsp;</font></u><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> that Borrower shall have no obligation to an Indemnitee hereunder with respect to Indemnified Liabilities directly resulting from the gross negligence or willful misconduct of that Indemnitee, as </font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" color=black lang=EN-US>determined by a court of competent jurisdiction by a final and nonappealable judgment</font><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US>.&nbsp; In no event shall any Lender and/or any of their respective employees, agents, partners, affiliates, members, equity and/or debt holders, managers, officers, directors and/or other related or similar type of Person, have any liability to the Borrower and/or any of its officers, directors, employees, agent, attorneys, affiliates, consultants, equity and/or debt holders except for any actions or lack of actions of such persons that are found by a court of competent jurisdiction after the time for all appeals has passed to have resulted directly from Lender&#146;s intentional misconduct or gross negligence.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; NOTHING HEREIN SHALL AFFECT THE LENDER&#146;S RIGHT TO SERVE PROCESS IN ANY OTHER MANNER PERMITTED BY LAW.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="Times New Roman" lang=EN-US> <p style="MARGIN-BOTTOM:0px; The Borrower will take all action that is appropriate or necessary to assure that its offerings of other securities will not be integrated for purposes of the 1933 Act or the rules and regulations of the Trading Market, with the issuance of Securities contemplated herein.</font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; From and after the date hereof and so long as the Note is outstanding, the Borrower, nor any of its respective officers, employees, directors, agents or other representatives, will, without the prior written consent of the Lender (which consent may be withheld, delayed or conditioned in the Lender&#146;s sole discretion), effect, enter into, announce or recommend to its stockholders any agreement, plan, arrangement or transaction (or issue, amend or waive any security) that would or would reasonably be expected to restrict, delay, conflict with or impair the ability or right of the Borrower to timely perform its obligations under the Documents. </font></p><font style="FONT-SIZE:11pt; MARGIN:0in 0in 12pt; TEXT-INDENT:0.5in"><a name=_aciFooter31> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal" face="times new roman" lang=EN-US>30</font></p> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0in 0in 0pt" align=center>&nbsp;</p></div></div> <hr size=1> <div style=PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:always>&nbsp;</div><a name=page_32> <div style="PADDING-LEFT:0%; PADDING-RIGHT:0%"><a name=_aciHeader32> <div> <p style="TEXT-ALIGN:right;
